< Review>
01/27/2021

** BEWARE -- This is not a place to take your vehicle, shady stuff going on. **

I had a groupon for a 4 wheel alignment. I called them yesterday and they stated to come in today at 2PM. When I got there, I was informed the internet was down and they could not complete the alignment. I have the ability to work remotely so I let them know i'll work from their lobby and if the internet comes up that is good, but if not, i'll return another day.

Towards the end of the day at 4:45PM, the technician comes back into the lobby and states the internet did not come back up and will have to try another day. I was ok with this as i took the chance of it not coming back up.

When I asked for my keys, the technician went into the garage to retrieve them and then told me that my front two windows are completely down and that it just started raining. I told him i NEVER leave my windows down especially on a rainy day. He then said... I'm just letting know as to imply that i left my windows down. The car was completely drenched on the inside. In addition, my two hubcaps on the passenger were not completely secured and they were just hanging on there partially secured.

I can't help but wonder 1) why did they put both windows down, 2) what work did they really do by taking the two hubcaps off and 3) there was no work authorization form completed? If their internet was down, there was no reason for them to even get in my vehicle....

I cancelled the groupon and will be taking my business elsewhere. I've always been the type of person to support local business, unfortunately this is not one of them.

** BEWARE -- This is not a place to take your vehicle, shady stuff going on. **< /Review>

5< /Rate>
< Review>
It is a very pleasant place to be. Not necessarily the Pacific Corinthian Yatch Club, but just being away from your home town, wherever that may be, is very invigorating. The California coast line is very beautiful. If you own a Yatch and rent slip then I guess it's the place to be, Unless you're already a member of another yatch club. It's a great place to be on the weekend especially if you've had  a very stressful work week. The coastline of California is a great place to decompress. Yatch clubs are just a part of the decompression process. Where do the locals go to decompress? Hopefully they have their own decompression techniques, or maybe living there is enough to keep anyone grounded.< /Review>

< Review>
Nov2020: it saddens me to have to change my review from a 5 star to a 1 star. I was happy to have a pho place so close to home that took pride in the food quality. We should've knew something was wrong when the restaurant was closed early on sunday. We decided to try again and noticed all the staff was changed, possible new owners? We still wanted to give them a chance, but was disappointed by the service. We ordered pho and sushi lunch and the pho arrived quick without any chopsticks or eating utensils. then were informed there was no fresh bean sprouts or basil. They offered carrots as a substitute, but that would change the whole composition of the flavor. We asked why they didn't tell us before the food arrived so we could order something else, we weren't given a answer and walked away. We then asked for the sushi lunch to go and we waited another 15 minutes till we realized the sushi was never made. Instead the owners just talked in the back, obviously not happy with our decision to not want an incomplete pho. I've never walked out from a restaurant in my life, but we weren't given much choice at that point.

March2020: Delicious broth, hearty portions and tasty sushi. Happy to have this place close to home. (Photos from this visit)<//Review>

<gmapID>0x80c326329aa2d119:0xc0ebc494de7ceebd< /gmapID><date>1459629723497</date><Resp>None< /Resp>< Rate>

<pictures>None</pictures>< text>
I took my son to children's choice for his first ever dental visit. As we arrived, we noticed that the building was new and modern which was nice compared to allot of dentist offices we've seen. When we walked in, nervous about taking our young child to the dentist because of our own horrible experiences, we were greeted by a smiling receptionist. She was very nice and helpful, and even offered us something to drink. Our son instantly ran to the wall of tablets set up for the kids to play with while we wait. They had tons of games on them for the kids of all ages to play. We only waited about 10 min's- top, even though the office was busy with lot's of other waiting families. It probably helped that I had my paperwork ready, printed from their website ahead of time and filled out before we arrived.

We were called back by a VERY nice dental assistant whom also was smiling-I don't know what her name was but she was a pretty young Latina, to a secondary waiting room, to await his ex rays. We waited about 5 more min's, and we were able to utilize their sink with their free tooth brush and tooth paste to brush his teeth before his ex rays.

When she called my son back to have his ex rays, he grabbed onto me and didn't want to go. The nice young Latina girl said to him "do you like movies?" and she asked him what movie he liked and told him she'd put it on for him. Instantly he let go of me and followed her. I thought to myself "BRILLIANT!", as I was a little teary eyed because I hate to make my son go this. It's absolutely brilliant that they do the movies for the kids. Bravo!

He sat through the ex rays for his first time with a smile on his face. That really made me and my husband relax. After ex rays, another very nice nurse took us to our spot for him to get his teeth cleaned and meet the Dentist. This nurse was an older Latina lady, smiling and kind just like the rest. She made my son feel comfortable, and me and my husband feel relaxed. Such a relief! I can't even tell you how relieving this is. My husband and I have never seen this at any dentist before. It was the best feeling to know our son was in good caring hands.

The dentist came out, a pretty young Asian lady. Again, she was smiling and kind. She explained to him what she was going to do, then she counted his teeth and examined them, she was very sweet to him and you can tell she was born to work with children. She reviewed his ex rays with us, and went over any concerns.

Then another very nice nurse a young black girl with braces and a beautiful smile that makes you smile, took us back to let our son pick out a balloon and a toy. What I call the cherry on top!

I could not be happier with our experience. My husband and I walked out of their almost shocked because we did not expect that. All our memories of the dentist were not good, and we were dreading taking our son. All those feelings are gone, and my son has been begging me to go back to the dentist. Wonderful!

Thank Children's Choice, God bless your entire staff. Your kindness, and understanding of children's fears and needs are outstanding! You definitely get my nomination for BEST Children's Dental Office! Keep up the good work, and we'll see you in 6 months!

< text>
This Williams Sonoma location is ground zero for wealthy Los Gatos foodies to congregate and shop for gorgeous high-end kitchen gadgetry, flatware, Shun knives and other fun stuff. While this shop is richly decorated, the aisles between merchandise are quite narrow. As you can expect, this makes for a crowded (but polite) scrum on weekends. The friendly clerks roam the aisles, and are always very proactive in making sure that your questions are answered - a mark of responsive customer service.<//text>

< text>
Pretty cool theatre that offers luxury movie watching experience. They have a restaurant inside where you can dine before or after your movie. You can also order items (food and or beverages) from your theatre seat and have them brought to you. Theatres are moderately sized so, not too big and not too small. Seats are nice and comfy. Plenty of leg room. Prices range from $18-36 per seat. Higher cost seats come with a blanket, pillow, reclining seats and food/drink service. If you are looking for something a step above or exclusive in your movie watching experience, Ipic is where it's at. Oh, and they do validate for parking.</text>

<Text>$64(!!!) for two movie tickets and about 11 pieces of popcorn, sodas are extra. While I want to like this place- because I believe in treating ourselves and enjoying some luxury- I just can't. I simply don't see the value. Now that most other theaters- AMC, Landmark etc- all have great reclining seats here you're basically paying DOUBLE for a blanket (they stopped the pillows) and a sample size taster of popcorn. In fact our seats didn't even have blankets today and the sachets of popcorn (I mean the bags really are provocatively tiny) arrived 30 mins(!) and two presses of the little service button later from our clearly very stressed and overworked server. iPic will tell you that what you're paying for is the option to have food and drinks served to you during the film. <rate>5<//rate>< text>
After an impromptu invitation to go and see a movie we decided to check out the iPic Theater which also had the Tuck Room connected to the theater.  The venue did have valet parking but we chose to do the validated parking which was only $3.30 for 4 hours which two me screams a deal compared to other parking places. We came in chose the movie and got the Supreme premium seats and then went over to grab a bite the prices were moderate at the tuck room. the food taste really great and everything paired Well together and you could tell that most of the drinks and the items on the menu have been thought out very well.

Our server then informed us that we were allowed to enter the theater 30 minutes before our show and that we could also order in the theater because of the premium seats and that these seats also came with complimentary popcorn.

The service was absolutely stellar we ordered chocolate chip toffee cookies french fries sliders and the complementary popcorn was really crunchy and fresh but kind of salty.

The movie theater held about 75 seats if even that. It was divided into two different sections Gray section and the yellow sections the yellow seats were recliners that came with a blanket and a little pillow of which you could also order food to be delivered to you from the yellows seated area.  The food came really quick and was really tasty along with the service they were moving in with ease without interrupting the movies for other.

Overall we had a great experience the bathroom was really spacious and it was also unisex there was also a convenient bar outside of the theater of which the bartender gave us some of the chef's on complimentary mixed nuts.

Just go check it out it's worth every bit of it we will definitely return.

Because I definitely. Would "Pic" this theater again, LOL see what I did there.< /text>

< text>
I LOVE iPic.  I'm so happy they opened a location in westwood - which is a bit closer to us then Pasadena.  Can we get one up in the valley now?! :)

The tickets are expensive but for a great date night when you know the movie will be good this is the place to go.

Spend the extra $10 and go for the fully reclining seats.  You get free unlimited popcorn, a pillow, and a blanket too.

The theaters are small and there isn't a bad seat in the house.  This is also a very fun place to go to with a big group of friends.

Come with your appetite. The food is also amazing.  We partook in lobster rolls and a panini.  The portions are small while the price is still high BUT the food was very good and had great quality.  We also realized that they probably want to serve small/normal portions so that you aren't uncomfortable or having to leave during the movie.

If you like alcohol, get the Marilyn Monroe lemonade!</text>

<Review>iPic has ruined movies in LA for me.  In the sense that I I refuse to go absolutely anywhere else to see a film...  I know there's other upscale super comfy theaters in LA, but to me iPic is the best.

Being a Sapphire member (a paid membership, worth every penny) gets you pretty clutch deals like pre-release tickets before anyone else, allowing me to secure myself some great seats to the most popular new releases.

Tuesdays are also member happy hour nights, with drink and food specials.

During the week, member prices are beyond reasonable, $18 a seat.  Equal to or better than any "regular" theater in LA.  Weekends however prices get jacked up pretty high, so I tend to stick to mid-week showings.  You also get free popcorn!!

The restaurant and bar (Tanzy) are also pretty on point.

Go, and you will never want to go elsewhere for a movie again.<//Review>< pictures>

<review>iPic had been on my list of LA things to do for a while, and I am so glad I finally went.

We arrived about 10 minutes before the movie we wanted to watch, to find it had been sold out. They fortunately had another movie we wanted to watch for a showtime about 40 minutes later. We had a comfortable wait in Tuck Room Tavern, examining the menu. No one bothers you to ask if you're going to order; they seem to understand that you may be waiting.

The cinema for your film opens about 30 minutes before the movie starts. I would recommend arriving early, given you get a chance to look at the menu and get comfortable with the chair, the blanket, and the pillow.

I loved it! Definitely on the expensive side, but what a great movie watching experience. Drinks and food were delicious, with unlimited popcorn. We ordered the homemade ginger beer, which was mango-habanero. Also loved the el corazon margarita (with pomegranate), and the truffle fries!

Service was very responsive. Granted, we were in the back where waiters could see us easily. Overall, may not do again because of the price but absolutely loved it.<//review><Rating>4<//Rating><Time>1481581810261<//Time>< user_name>
Prerna Gupta< /user_name>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
I'd never been to one of these dine-in movie theaters but a very generous friend invited me out for an evening of movie pampering and I was excited to check it out! It sure isn't cheap (we even got the upgraded deluxe seats for $10 extra, woohoo), but I believe you get your money's worth in smoothly reclining leather seats, blanket and pillow, bag of popcorn, and chairside wait service for food and drinks. The food was good (if not outstanding) in my opinion (we tried their hummus plate and a flatbread pizza), but the service was great, from the ticket people to the wait staff, everyone was uniformly friendly and solicitous. I was also impressed with the luxe decor and sophisticated art on the walls--it's got a great ambiance. This is definitely one of those "Treat. Yo. Self." places and I'll be sure to return on occasion when I just don't feel like dealing with the rabble.<//review>

Stephanie Han<//Name>

< text>
I've been to both AMC and IPic and I love them both for different reasons. I loved being treated as  an adult  and not just another movie goer at the IPic. Nice leather recliners. A wonderful glass of wine.  Most importantly, the quiet; no rustling of popcorn. Yes, AMC is cheaper, but it's just a movie house. IPic is so much more. I am willing to pay the extra price for the service, and adult atmosphere when I can afford to do so.<//text>

<user_name>Gene Rukavina</user_name>< Rate>
2</Rate>
< review>
Okay, so I resisted giving just one star, based on the fact that I really used to love the iPic in Westwood. It used to be a 4-5 star experience and worth the extra money. Sadly, the iPic Westowwod location seems to be off the rails these days.

I was there with my girlfriend to see Cinderella on Sunday 4/12/15. As a Sapphire member, I would expect to be notified by email if there are any significant changes to the perks of membership. So I was quite surprised to learn that the self-parking fee was no longer covered for members when I arrived to check in for the movie. Seriously? When did this happen? This is not a good sign when the parking fee can no longer be covered as a membership benefit. Especially when you consider how much more it costs for the experience itself! Once we arrived to our seats, we were surprised to find no iPad/tablet at all, just the fixture that used to hold it! Instead, there was an actual menu sitting on the table. This is how it was at the very beginning when this location first opened, so it seems like things are regressing! What is even worse, is that these obviously old menus don't even list everything that had been listed in the tablet system. As a beer drinker, I know they offer that, but it was nowhere to be found on the menu. Worst of all, is the obvious decline in service once you get to your seat. That is really the whole point of paying extra for an iPic experience. Sure, the reclining chairs with the blanket and pillow are nice, but without prompt service, the experience is ruined. In the past we received fast service and there appeared to be more than one server working in the theater. On this occasion there seemed to be just one server working the entire theater. There seemed to be one other person that only delivered popcorn. Needless to say, it took forever for the server to finally get to us. By this point we had lost our desire to order any food since we could not trust when it would actually arrive so we settled for beer and wine instead. When the popcorn arrived, the quality was clearly not as good as we had remembered from past experiences and it was very salty! I could not enjoy my popcorn because I had to wait so long for my first drink to arrive.

This is not the iPic experience that I have come to expect. I am now seriously considering how I can cancel my membership and I am seriously doubting whether or not I want to shell out the extra money ($50 for the two CInderella tickets) in the future. So sad to see such a great concept run in to the ground in our neighborhood. I also tried contacting via the website, but have yet to hear back. :(</review>
